      <h5><a href="http://newsroom.ucr.edu/2843">Bilayer Graphene Works as an Insulator</a></h5> 
      <h6>24-Jan-2012</h6> 
      <p>Jeanie Lau's lab has identified a property of bilayer graphene that she says is analogous to finding the Higgs boson in particle physics.</p>

     <div id="omnicontent"> 
      <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="home-image" group="Everyone" button="727" -->
      <!-- com.omniupdate.editor toolbar="IMG_ONLY" csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="484" -->
      <p><img src="/images/cbnsbanner.jpg" alt="CBNS Banner" /></p>

      <!-- ouc:editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="484"/ -->
      <p style="text-align: justify;">Research in the Department of Cell Biology and Neuroscience uses multidisciplinary approaches to understanding basic cellular processes in various tissues, including the nervous system, as well as more integrative levels of analysis, including behavior. Areas of research represented in the department include the following:</p> 
      <ul class="checkboxes, tight"> 
       <li class="tight, checked">Biophysical properties of excitable membranes</li> 
       <li class="tight, checked">DNA repair</li> 
       <li class="tight, checked">Transcriptional regulation</li> 
       <li class="tight, checked">Mechanisms of toxicity</li> 
       <li class="tight, checked">Insect development</li> 
       <li class="tight, checked">Membrane transport</li> 
       <li class="tight, checked">Mechanisms of mitotic chromosome transmission</li> 
       <li class="tight, checked">Telomere maintenance</li> 
       <li class="tight, checked">Synaptic structure and function</li> 
       <li class="tight, checked">Changes in nervous system with experience</li> 
       <li class="tight, checked">Interactions of nervous and endocrine systems</li> 
       <li class="tight, checked">Reproductive biology and fertilization</li> 
       <li class="tight, checked">Chemokine function in wound healing and tumor development</li> 
       <li class="tight, checked">Glia-neuron signaling</li> 
       <li class="tight, checked">Brainstem and spinal cord control of locomotion</li> 
      </ul> 
      <h3>Undergraduate Curriculum</h3> 
      <p style="text-align: justify;">Students interested in cell, molecular, and developmental biology can obtain training through the interdepartmental <strong>Cell, Molecular, and Developmental Biology major</strong>&nbsp;leading to the B.S. degree. Students interested in neuroscience can obtain training in behavioral neuroscience, neurobiology, and neurochemistry through the <strong>Neuroscience major</strong> leading to the B.A. or B.S. degree. The Neuroscience major is an intercollege major offered by the College of Humanities, Arts, and Social Sciences and the College of Natural and Agricultural Sciences.</p> 
      <h3>Graduate Curriculum</h3> 
      <p style="text-align: justify;">Courses and research opportunities are offered by the interdepartmental graduate programs in the following fields:</p> 
      <ul class="star"> 
       <li><a href="http://cmdb.ucr.edu/" target="_blank">Cell, Molecular and Developmental Biology</a></li> 
       <li><a href="http://etox.ucr.edu/" target="_blank">Environmental Toxicology</a></li> 
       <li><a href="http://ggb.ucr.edu/" target="_blank">Genetics</a></li> 
       <li><a href="http://microbiology.ucr.edu/" target="_blank">Microbiology</a></li> 
       <li><a href="http://neuro.ucr.edu/">Neuroscience</a></li> 
      </ul>

              <h2 class="branded-page-module-title"> <a href="/playlist?list=PLn9gUqW6huXVtpoO2CgevGimk2dLIkKM8" class="yt-uix-sessionlink branded-page-module-title-link spf-nolink" data-sessionlink="ei=qZMfU4vwD-Gn-AOX3YGgDA"> <span class="branded-page-module-title-text"> <span class="">A Cluttered Life: Middle-Class Abundance</span> </span> </a> <a href="/watch?v=KmUyTauQBQ4&amp;list=PLn9gUqW6huXVtpoO2CgevGimk2dLIkKM8" class="yt-uix-button  shelves-play yt-uix-sessionlink yt-uix-button-default yt-uix-button-size-small" data-sessionlink="ei=qZMfU4vwD-Gn-AOX3YGgDA"><span class="yt-uix-button-icon-wrapper"><img class="yt-uix-button-icon yt-uix-button-icon-play-all" src="http://s.ytimg.com/yts/img/pixel-vfl3z5WfW.gif" alt="" title="" /></span><span class="yt-uix-button-content">Play </span></a> </h2> 
              <div class="shelf-description yt-ui-ellipsis yt-ui-ellipsis-2">
                Americans sure do like their stuff. The problem is, it piles up, leaving families surrounded by overstuffed cabinets and plenty of clutter. This UCTV Prime series follows a team of UCLA anthropologists as they venture into the stuffed-to-capacity homes of dual income, middle class American families in order to truly understand the food, toys, and clutter that fill them.
               <br />http://www.uctv.tv/clutter

              <h2 class="branded-page-module-title"> <a href="/playlist?list=PLn9gUqW6huXW_fnJaRqf0ixZy7R5XNsl1" class="yt-uix-sessionlink branded-page-module-title-link spf-nolink" data-sessionlink="ei=qZMfU4vwD-Gn-AOX3YGgDA"> <span class="branded-page-module-title-text"> <span class="">Going Places: UC Education Abroad</span> </span> </a> <a href="/watch?v=dlJ9wXeoaKM&amp;list=PLn9gUqW6huXW_fnJaRqf0ixZy7R5XNsl1" class="yt-uix-button  shelves-play yt-uix-sessionlink yt-uix-button-default yt-uix-button-size-small" data-sessionlink="ei=qZMfU4vwD-Gn-AOX3YGgDA"><span class="yt-uix-button-icon-wrapper"><img class="yt-uix-button-icon yt-uix-button-icon-play-all" src="http://s.ytimg.com/yts/img/pixel-vfl3z5WfW.gif" alt="" title="" /></span><span class="yt-uix-button-content">Play </span></a> </h2> 
              <div class="shelf-description yt-ui-ellipsis yt-ui-ellipsis-2">
                From witnessing history at the Berlin Wall to saving lives in a remote West African community, this UCTV Prime series shares the life-changing stories of participants in the University of California's pioneering education abroad program. As the program marks 50 years of educating and inspiring global citizens, this series explores how UC study abroad students are influencing the world - and how the world is changing them.

             <div class="compact-shelf shelf-item yt-uix-shelfslider yt-uix-shelfslider-at-head yt-uix-shelfslider-at-tail vve-check clearfix branded-page-box yt-section-hover-container fluid-shelf yt-uix-tdl" data-sessionlink="ved=CMwBENwcKAQ&amp;ei=qZMfU4vwD-Gn-AOX3YGgDA"> 
              <h2 class="branded-page-module-title"> <a href="/playlist?list=PLn9gUqW6huXVIrvhfPhFn3BfwnGGEzYVF" class="yt-uix-sessionlink branded-page-module-title-link spf-nolink" data-sessionlink="ei=qZMfU4vwD-Gn-AOX3YGgDA"> <span class="branded-page-module-title-text"> <span class="">Museum Meets Orchestra</span> </span> </a> <a href="/watch?v=hzSgwo6pPdA&amp;list=PLn9gUqW6huXVIrvhfPhFn3BfwnGGEzYVF" class="yt-uix-button  shelves-play yt-uix-sessionlink yt-uix-button-default yt-uix-button-size-small" data-sessionlink="ei=qZMfU4vwD-Gn-AOX3YGgDA"><span class="yt-uix-button-icon-wrapper"><img class="yt-uix-button-icon yt-uix-button-icon-play-all" src="http://s.ytimg.com/yts/img/pixel-vfl3z5WfW.gif" alt="" title="" /></span><span class="yt-uix-button-content">Play </span></a> </h2> 
              <div class="shelf-description yt-ui-ellipsis yt-ui-ellipsis-2">
                UCLA's Hammer Museum invited wild Up, a 24-member, experimental classical/contemporary orchestra, to be in residence over a six-month period in 2012. During that time, the orchestra presented three major concerts and 30 smaller chamber music performances that defied convention and transformed the museum into a space as unexpected and moving as the music itself. This UCTV Prime original series, premiering January 2013, goes the behind-the-scenes of this unusual residency.
               <br />http://www.uctv.tv/museum-meets-orchestra 
              </div>

              <h2 class="branded-page-module-title"> <a href="/playlist?list=PLn9gUqW6huXUsW2WFd9qfDXGRPoSzQa9t" class="yt-uix-sessionlink branded-page-module-title-link spf-nolink" data-sessionlink="ei=qZMfU4vwD-Gn-AOX3YGgDA"> <span class="branded-page-module-title-text"> <span class="">Lifting the Blanket: Pursuit of a Climate Change Solution</span> </span> </a> <a href="/watch?v=WFzOh298-6k&amp;list=PLn9gUqW6huXUsW2WFd9qfDXGRPoSzQa9t" class="yt-uix-button  shelves-play yt-uix-sessionlink yt-uix-button-default yt-uix-button-size-small" data-sessionlink="ei=qZMfU4vwD-Gn-AOX3YGgDA"><span class="yt-uix-button-icon-wrapper"><img class="yt-uix-button-icon yt-uix-button-icon-play-all" src="http://s.ytimg.com/yts/img/pixel-vfl3z5WfW.gif" alt="" title="" /></span><span class="yt-uix-button-content">Play </span></a> </h2> 
              <div class="shelf-description yt-ui-ellipsis yt-ui-ellipsis-2">
                Beginning his career as an engineer at a refrigeration plant in India, Veerabhadran Ramanathan went on to make one of the most important climate change discoveries when he identified chlorofluorocarbons (CFCs) as even larger contributors to global warming than the previously identified culprit, carbon dioxide.
               <br />
               <br />This four-part series follows the Scripps Institution of Oceanography scientist's remarkable path that changed the face of climate change research and has introduced possibilities for human-scale solutions.
               <br />http://www.uctv.tv/lifting-the-blanket 
              </div>

              <h2 class="branded-page-module-title"> <a href="/playlist?list=PLn9gUqW6huXWZ7ZUTXeqZD7HzYJVhgmJn" class="yt-uix-sessionlink branded-page-module-title-link spf-nolink" data-sessionlink="ei=qZMfU4vwD-Gn-AOX3YGgDA"> <span class="branded-page-module-title-text"> <span class="">9 Billion Mouths to Feed: The Future of Farming</span> </span> </a> <a href="/watch?v=dlnrvkzEv9w&amp;list=PLn9gUqW6huXWZ7ZUTXeqZD7HzYJVhgmJn" class="yt-uix-button  shelves-play yt-uix-sessionlink yt-uix-button-default yt-uix-button-size-small" data-sessionlink="ei=qZMfU4vwD-Gn-AOX3YGgDA"><span class="yt-uix-button-icon-wrapper"><img class="yt-uix-button-icon yt-uix-button-icon-play-all" src="http://s.ytimg.com/yts/img/pixel-vfl3z5WfW.gif" alt="" title="" /></span><span class="yt-uix-button-content">Play </span></a> </h2> 
              <div class="shelf-description yt-ui-ellipsis yt-ui-ellipsis-2">
                The global population is expected to hit 9 billion by 2050 and there's an urgent need to reform our food production to meet the rising demand. This four-part series examines these challenges and demonstrates how UC Davis is leading the way in developing sustainable, high-tech agriculture practices and training the next generation of farmers.
               <br />http://www.uctv.tv/farming

              <h2 class="branded-page-module-title"> <a href="/playlist?list=PLn9gUqW6huXUr-6vc0qHfVyC7FWuy4-e0" class="yt-uix-sessionlink branded-page-module-title-link spf-nolink" data-sessionlink="ei=qZMfU4vwD-Gn-AOX3YGgDA"> <span class="branded-page-module-title-text"> <span class="">Lighting the World: Shuji Nakamura's Brilliant Discovery</span> </span> </a> <a href="/watch?v=hwz-rpcnqoU&amp;list=PLn9gUqW6huXUr-6vc0qHfVyC7FWuy4-e0" class="yt-uix-button  shelves-play yt-uix-sessionlink yt-uix-button-default yt-uix-button-size-small" data-sessionlink="ei=qZMfU4vwD-Gn-AOX3YGgDA"><span class="yt-uix-button-icon-wrapper"><img class="yt-uix-button-icon yt-uix-button-icon-play-all" src="http://s.ytimg.com/yts/img/pixel-vfl3z5WfW.gif" alt="" title="" /></span><span class="yt-uix-button-content">Play </span></a> </h2> 
              <div class="shelf-description yt-ui-ellipsis yt-ui-ellipsis-2">
                http://www.uctv.tv/light
               <br />We take light for granted, but more than two billion people in the world go through their entire lives without reliable lighting. But that is changing, thanks in part to the brilliant discovery of UC Santa Barbara's Shuji Nakamura.
               <br />
               <br />This four-part series, made possible by UC Santa Barbara's Solid State Lighting and Energy Center, tells the story of Nakamura's determined effort to develop the white LED and the revolution in lighting that his discovery has brought to the world. 
              </div>
